# Orchestrator event log (append-only)

The exact, chronological record of process + state — the zero-loss spine. **Append-only: never
rewrite or delete a line.** Every event (commit, user direction, decision, established
definition, recorded gap, correction) gets one line at the time it happens. A fresh session
reconstructs the exact process by reading this top-to-bottom; `git log` is the parallel
substrate for code, and `ORCHESTRATOR-STATE.md` is the derived synthesis (current position,
pending, conventions) — both reproducible from this log + git.

Entry format: `ISO-8601 (Asia/Shanghai) · TYPE · text · [refs]`
Types: COMMIT · DIRECTION (user) · DECISION · DEFINITION · GAP · ASSESSMENT · CORRECTION · STATE

Epoch: this log begins at the Phase-15 data-population round (2026-05-20). Prior history
(Phases 0–14, all commits) is in `git log` and the per-phase commit map in `ORCHESTRATOR-STATE.md`.

---

- 2026-05-22T09:15 · DECISION · Rename split (Pass A of the DEC-13/14 plan): `makemigrations` produced a destructive `DeleteModel`/`CreateModel`+`RemoveField`/`AddField` because renaming the model AND its targeting FK fields in one autodetector run defeats both heuristics; drop/create is unacceptable (seeded school rows). Chosen path (plan-approved): hand-author the rename ops (`RenameModel`+`RenameField`) and let Django generate the non-rename residual (AlterField/AlterModelOptions/constraint). First repo use of `RenameModel`/`RenameField` (no anti-precedent; the one prior "rename", school/0020, was a data-value change).
- 2026-05-22T09:25 · CORRECTION · IMPL surfaced a spec deficiency in the orchestrator directive (mandate-008, stopped not guessed): the test gate runs SQLite (`config/settings/test.py`), where `RenameField` remakes the whole table and replays the still-present `assignment_target_matches_kind` CheckConstraint whose `Q` still referenced `department` → `FieldError` building the test DB (Postgres `RENAME COLUMN` would cascade; SQLite does not). Fix: `RemoveConstraint(assignment_target_matches_kind)` ordered as the first op in plans/0022 (ahead of the rename); the generated plans/0023 re-adds it with the `division` predicate. Harmless on Postgres.

- 2026-05-22T14:55 · STOP (orchestrator, pre-Slice-8) · Slice 8 (US-ONB-2 first-login set-password) exposes a security fork the approved blueprint under-specified: the blueprint's "show the activation/set-password link on-screen at signup_done" is unsafe on a PUBLIC endpoint — displaying a set-password token for an entered email either reveals account existence (enumeration) or, for an existing account, hands an attacker a password-set link (account takeover). Secure delivery of a set-password token to an anonymous user requires email (proves ownership), OR the flow must set the password in-session, OR self-service is dropped in favor of admin-distributed links (CSV path only). Surfaced to user for a decision before building Slice 8; Slice 7 (account genesis) stands.

- 2026-05-26T10:45 · DISCOVERY (user-surfaced, recorded) · DISC-22-0526-A — **responsibility is division-grained but responsibilities are role-borne**. Surfaced by the user during the DEC-32 build (the SAO org question → "positions can't carry atomic responsibilities ... the elaboration of possible responsibilities and roles ... can't be exactly articulated"). Two prongs: (1) `Assignment` has no `position` target (accountable party = division | optional person, no role rung) → SAO-pastoral steps collapse to "SAO" (no sub-divisions; YGL/HRT are Positions); (2) DEC-32's `DivisionResponsibility` atoms hang off Division ONLY → a Position (a future dorm-supervisor vs a YGL) cannot carry its own responsibility atoms → role-specific responsibilities within a division aren't articulable. The plan-decomposition (US-LLM-24) + the responsibility-fulfillment assist (US-LLM-27) reason over a too-coarse grain. RESOLUTION DIRECTION (shape OPEN): make responsibility position-grained as well as division-grained — `PositionResponsibility` (parallel to DivisionResponsibility) OR a generalized `Responsibility`(division-or-position owner); + `Assignment.position`; + extend the DEC-32 `ActionStepResponsibility` linkage + grounding to the position grain. Division-level atoms stay valid (office-wide purview) — they EXTEND, not waste. Faithful to DISC-16 (YGL/HRT deliberately positions, not units; does NOT require year-group/homeroom sub-divisions). **SEQUENCING: settle BEFORE US-LLM-27** (the responsibility-fulfillment assist must reason/link at the right grain) — i.e. this gates/precedes US-LLM-27 in the DEC-32 follow-on. Persisted: DISC-22 in `phases/discoveries.md` (OPEN) + this line + STATE open-discovery pointer. No code; analysis/record only — the model shape is the user's open decision (think-out, then a plan→impl). Connects to DEC-32 (revises the atom grain) + the earlier-mentioned `Assignment.position` rung (now subsumed here as prong 1).
- 2026-05-26T11:00 · DECISION (user) · DISC-22 shape NARROWED — **dedicated `PositionResponsibility`, NOT a polymorphic owner**. User rejected the "generalized `Responsibility` whose owner is a division OR a position" option: "Positions have responsibilities. Responsibilities don't stay the same for position" — i.e. responsibilities are owned by a position as a first-class thing, and a division-responsibility vs a position-responsibility are DIFFERENT kinds of thing (each position has its own distinct set), not one generic entity floating between owners. So the resolution shape is **two dedicated, parallel models**: `DivisionResponsibility` (built, Layer 1 — office-wide purview, UNTOUCHED) + a NEW `PositionResponsibility` (FK position, statement, order — each position's own atoms; dorm-supervisor's set ≠ YGL's set). Purely ADDITIVE (no rework of the division-level atoms). The rest of the DISC-22 resolution stands: `Assignment.position` (the role rung) + extend the DEC-32 `ActionStepResponsibility` linkage + grounding to the position grain; settle before US-LLM-27. - 2026-05-26T12:40 · DECISION (user) · DEC-35 — **HOD is modeled as a `Position` under the subject-department `Division`, complementary to `Division.head`.** Resolves the head-vs-position question surfaced after DISC-22. User: "HOD responsibilities are meant to be part of the allocatable inventory the orchestration reasons over (US-LLM-24/27); the HOD needs a Position representation under the subject-dept division, not only the head FK." Rationale: `Division.head` (FK→Person) is a bare org-leader pointer — no `PositionResponsibility` atoms, and `Assignment` has no "head" target (only division/position, DISC-22) → an HOD modeled only as `head` cannot carry role-specific responsibility atoms, cannot enter the DISC-22 division+position responsibility INVENTORY, and cannot be the responsible party on a step at the HOD grain. Decision: represent the HOD as a `Position` (a "Head of Department" seat) under each subject-dept `Division` (children of C&T), carrying `PositionResponsibility` atoms (= its job description, DEC-29) and `Assignment.position`-assignable so US-LLM-24/27 allocate it. COMPLEMENTARY not redundant ("not only the head FK"): `Division.head` retained as the rollup leader-pointer (`people_in_subtree`, `Person.heads`); the HOD `Position` is the responsibility-bearing seat; a dept leader is linked BOTH ways (head FK + a `Holding` of the HOD Position). **NO model change** — Position + PositionResponsibility + Assignment.position + grounding positions-nesting all exist (DISC-22 `a38c561`); the grounding inventory picks up the HOD automatically once the Position rows + atoms exist as data. Supersedes the `docs/domain-model.md` Position-entry prior art ("an HOD is not a position — it is the head"), corrected this turn. SCOPE narrow (the HOD/subject-dept case named); the same mechanism is already DISC-22-supported for any other division head, but that is the user's call when it arises (not prescribed). Follow-on build (own plan→impl; orchestrator-direct seed): a data migration creating an HOD `Position` under each of the 5 seeded subject departments, keyed (division,label) per the get_or_create seed convention; its responsibility atoms are admin-authored content (owed). Seed details to settle at seed time (content, not structure): the label convention (uniform "Head of Department" vs per-subject) + whether atoms are a shared role description or per-dept. People-linking (head FK + HOD Holding) needs the roster — D7-blocked; the Position+atoms seed independently. No new US story minted (mechanism + admin editing already exist; no augmentation). Persisted: DEC-35 (data/seed-round-plan.md) + docs/domain-model.md (Position entry + Division.head note) + this line + STATE.

- 2026-05-26T18:00 · COMMITS (IMPL `51ff5cd` + `363454f`) + cleavage carry-forward item 1 BUILT+VERIFIED · **Locale-neutral `Person` name structure shipped, with project-wide modeltranslation fallback fix as the dev-DB-verify-exposed follow-on.** Two code commits this work-block:
  - `51ff5cd` (Person refactor): replaced `Person.name` (single translated CharField) with four locale-neutral fields — `family_name` / `given_name` / `display_name` (all Latin, untranslated) + `name_native` (translated; `_en` + `_zh_hans` columns). New `__str__` fallback chain: `display_name` → `f"{given_name} {family_name}".strip()` → `name_native` → `f"Person #{pk}"`. New `Meta.ordering = ["family_name", "given_name"]`. `PersonAdmin.list_display` / `search_fields` updated. Translation registration swap (drop `name`, add `name_native`). One schema migration `school/0043_person_name_refactor` (6 AddField + 3 RemoveField + 1 AlterModelOptions; reversible; safe — 0 Person rows on dev DB). ~30 test-fixture callsites mechanically updated (`name="X Y"` → `family_name="Y", given_name="X"` pattern); new positive coverage on `__str__` fallback chain + translation round-trip + ordering. `User` auth model UNTOUCHED (separate scope). No business code reads `Person.name` directly (only `__str__`); AI grounding does not emit Person names; no plans/school FK changes needed.
  - `363454f` (project-wide fallback fix): dev-DB verification of `51ff5cd` exposed a defect — `Person.__str__`'s `self.name_native` read is the modeltranslation **active-language proxy**, which returns empty when only `_zh_hans` has content under EN-active context (default), so a Chinese-only Person rendered `"Person #N"` instead of `"方苑苑"`. **Project-wide audit (Explore) found the SAME bug pattern in 32 of 47 `__str__` methods** across school + plans (Position, Division, DivisionResponsibility, Plan, Phase, Milestone, ActionStep, SubStep, Communication, Evidence, FeedbackChannel, ReviewEvent, RevisionRule, SuccessCriterion, StatementClause, every reference-vocab label-bearing model, School.name itself). Root cause: no `MODELTRANSLATION_FALLBACK_LANGUAGES` setting → library defaults to no auto-fallback. Fix: ONE config line in `config/settings/base.py` — `MODELTRANSLATION_FALLBACK_LANGUAGES = ("en", "zh-hans")`. Bidirectional symmetric cascade (active-language column first, then walk tuple in order until non-empty). Read-only — no save behavior change, no `.filter()` change. **Per mandate-004 a Person-only fix would have been negligent** (31 other models silently broken when the root-cause fix is one line). Tests: simplified the existing `test_str_falls_back_to_name_native_when_latin_blank` to drop the workaround that set both base + `_zh_hans` (now sets only `_zh_hans` and asserts surfacing); new `test_str_falls_back_to_name_native_when_chinese_active` proves the symmetric reverse under `override("zh-hans")`; new `school/tests/test_translation_fallback.py` proves the fix is project-wide via Position + DivisionResponsibility regression assertions. No `__str__` code change in any of the 32 sites — the settings fix obsoletes per-model workarounds.
  
  **Process notes (mandate-007 / -004 transparency):** the original `51ff5cd` test passed because it used the base `name_native=` field directly (which under EN-active populates both `_en` and the base) — masking the bug; the dev-DB probe under realistic per-language-column authoring exposed it. The fix path was decided by Explore audit (32 affected sites) → root cause (one config line) rather than localized patching. **One process error this work-block:** the IMPL subagent for `51ff5cd` applied `school/0043` to the dev DB during its run (orchestrator territory; idempotent + verified). Also: a transient AskUserQuestion was sent to the user that proliferated options when the path was settled (saved as memory `feedback-options-proliferation-noise`); recovered to single-path plan.
  
  **Gate re-run independent (orchestrator):** check 0; makemigrations No changes; ruff baseline-only (6 pre-existing, zero new across both commits); ruff format 394 clean; mypy Success **283 source files** (+1 from `test_translation_fallback.py`); pytest **1438 passed** (+7 vs. US-LLM-27's 1431 baseline: 4 new from `51ff5cd`'s test_person.py expansions, 1 chinese-active fallback test, 2 project-wide regression tests); make test-js **42** unchanged. **Dev DB:** `school/0043` applied + verified — six new cols present (`family_name`, `given_name`, `display_name`, `name_native`, `name_native_en`, `name_native_zh_hans`), three old cols dropped (`name`, `name_en`, `name_zh_hans`); Person `__str__` 4-path round-trip now ALL correct (path 1 display=`Celestine`; path 2 given+family=`Yuanyuan Fang`; path 3 zh_hans-only=`方苑苑`; path 4 pk-defensive=`Person #N`); Position `label_zh_hans`-only renders `数学教师 (...)`; DivisionResponsibility `statement_zh_hans`-only renders `按时检查作业`. **Cleavage carry-forward item 1 (`docs/tenant-vs-generic-cleavage.md`) → BUILT + VERIFIED.** Items 2–5 (DEC-35 generalization, YearGroup model, `tenant_chiway` app, optional AccreditationBody parent) remain pending user validation. **Working-tree note:** `data/school-content-intake-2026-05-26.md` carries uncommitted user edits + the staff roster CSV `data/may-27-2026-staff-names-crs.csv` remains untracked — both user-owned working surfaces, not orchestrator-committable.

- 2026-05-29T15:45 · DEVIATION SURFACED — DEC-39 ENFORCEMENT IS STRUCTURALLY INCOMPLETE (mandate-007/008 — sub-agent surfaced; orchestrator forwards) · **The three landed commits expand `grounding_include` tuples, inject the no-fabrication preamble into all 14 production bodies, insert per-spec free-text-tightening clauses, and sync the workshop — BUT the snippet bodies + production bodies DO NOT render the newly-grounded catalogues into the prompt text via `{% if <section> %}{% for x in <section> %}- {{ x.label }}{% endfor %}{% endif %}` blocks.** Concretely, F1's snippet (and the corresponding production body) now has the line "Every actor, unit, role, position-title, or owning body named in `description` or `assessment` MUST be a verbatim match to a Division or Position label from the divisions catalogue above; every stakeholder named MUST be a label from the stakeholder_groups catalogue; every policy named MUST be a label from the policies catalogue" — but no divisions catalogue, no stakeholder_groups catalogue, no policies catalogue is rendered above. The grounding bundle `build_grounding(school, draft_state, include=spec.grounding_include)` correctly assembles the data into the context dict at render time; Django's `Template(body).render(Context(grounding))` renders ONLY what `{% if %}` / `{% for %}` blocks invoke; nothing in F1's body (or B1's, A1's, F4's, F5's, US-LLM-27's, A2's, G1's, F3's) iterates the newly-grounded sections; the LLM receives a stricter directive without the enumerated lists the directive points to. **Fabrication risk persists at the same joints** — possibly worse (the LLM now has an explicit "draw from catalogue X above" rule and no catalogue X to draw from, which may push it to refuse, half-fill, or invent harder to comply with the directive surface). The user's directive ("such that we never run into invention again") is NOT MET by the three landed commits alone. **Canonical resolution path** (the only mandate-compliant fix): a fourth IMPL slice that adds `{% if <section> %}{% for x in <section> %}- {{ x.label }} ...{% endfor %}{% endif %}` rendering blocks to each affected snippet body AND a follow-on `ai/0019_render_no_fabrication_catalogues.py` migration mirroring the additions to the 9 affected production PromptTemplate bodies. The block shapes per section: `divisions` → iterate nested positions per division (the `_divisions` emitter at `ai/services/grounding.py:195` already nests positions+responsibility-atoms; full Division+Position+atom enumeration is one iteration); `stakeholder_groups` / `policies` / `accreditation_standards` / `learner_outcomes` / `mission_areas` / `areas_for_improvement` / `guiding_statements` / `frequencies` / `cycle` / `year_groups` → simple `{% for %}` over the catalogue. - 2026-05-30T09:45 · DEC-42 ESTABLISHED — FREE-TEXT FABRICATION AUDIT SHIFTS FROM AD-HOC REGEX EXTRACTION TO NLP NOUN-PHRASE CHUNKER (user directive: "update all our updatable context so next session knows exactly the focus: 1. Replace the ad-hoc regex with an NLP noun-phrase chunker") · Formalizes the architectural decision to abandon the incremental punctuation-class patching pattern (documented across DISC-29 + DISC-31's 5 classes + DISC-32 colon-boundary) and replace `_freetext_audit.py::extract_proper_name_spans` with a real NLP noun-phrase chunker (spaCy / NLTK / similar). **Rationale**: the LLM prose-pattern space is too large to enumerate boundary-by-boundary via regex; each empirical re-dispatch surfaces a new edge class; the asymptote of the incremental approach is finite-but-never-zero. NLP noun-phrase chunking is a long-solved problem; punctuation boundaries (commas, colons, semicolons, parens, em-dashes, en-dashes, slashes, ellipses, sentence terminators, possessives) come for free from a mature library. The catalogue lookup logic (`CatalogueUnion::admits`, `KNOWN_GENERIC_TERMS`) stays unchanged — only the extraction stage swaps. **Engineering shape**: single dependency addition to `school-improvement-plans/pyproject.toml` + rewrite of `extract_proper_name_spans` + migration of existing regression fixtures + gate run. Small investment, comprehensive closure. **Resolves**: DISC-29 (single-token gap), DISC-32 (colon-boundary), and the entire future-tail of punctuation-boundary defect classes in ONE landing — supersedes DISC-31's incremental-patching closure direction (the 5 closed classes remain valid but the underlying approach evolves). **Alternatives considered + rejected**: option 2 (restructure every spec's OUTPUT CONTRACT to typed entity fields + templated prose) is corpus-wide redesign — kept as longer-term consideration; option 3 (verifier LLM secondary pass) is probabilistic, doesn't meet structural fabrication-impossibility goal — rejected. **Project pattern alignment**: consistent with DEC-32 / DEC-39 / DEC-40 / DEC-41 — admin-curated catalogue is still the source of truth, parser is still the structural enforcement gate; only the noun-phrase extraction stage swaps from incremental-regex-patching to library-provided extraction. Per DEC-41 the fix lands once and benefits both workshop iteration and Django service dispatch (production parser uses the same module). NOT a model change, NOT a migration; pure Python module rewrite + dependency addition. **Persistence**: this DEC + DISC-29 + DISC-32 closure-path-settled annotations + this LOG event + STATE refresh recording NEXT-SESSION FOCUS = implement DEC-42; all in this tracking commit per persistence-in-same-turn discipline. **Cross-references**: DISC-29 + DISC-31 + DISC-32 (the empirical-patching trail this DEC-42 supersedes); DEC-39 + DEC-40 (the fabrication-closure pattern this extends); DEC-41 (workshop ↔ production framing — the fix lands at the Python module level, benefits both modes).

- 2026-05-30T11:00 · DEC-43 ESTABLISHED — FREE-TEXT AUDIT REFRAMES AS CLOSED-SET ENTITY LINKING + OUTLIER DETECTION (user direction: "encode option E as the decision and proceed with canonical pipeline and status updating") · Supersedes DEC-42's specific extraction-API direction (`doc.noun_chunks`); DEC-42's principle ("library-provided extraction replaces ad-hoc regex patching") stands. The catalogue per tenant is a closed admin-curated set (~200 labels) known at parse time; this is the wrong abstraction for any noun-phrase parser.
